<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточивать.html>сосредото́чивать</a> (30752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточить.html>сосредото́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sosredotóčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточивать.html>сосредото́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosredotóčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточить.html>сосредото́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to concentrate, to fix, to focus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточивать.html>сосредото́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sosredotóčivatʹ</b> vnimánije (na)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to concentrate one's attention (on, upon)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосредоточивать.html>сосредото́чивающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosredotóčivajuščij</span>)

***состав.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́в</a> (1018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sostáv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>composition, structure, membership, staff, body
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́ве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>sostáve</b> čevó</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">as a part of, composed of</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> composition, solution, mixture</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> train, stock</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sostávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to constitute, to make up, to form</li>
<li>to compose, to construct, to draw up, to prepare
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вить</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резюме.html>резюме́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak <b>sostávitʹ</b>/<b>sostavljátʹ</b> rezjumɛ́?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How should one prepare a résumé?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to place objects on top of each other to form a stack</li>
<li>to move things from one place to another
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вим</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:посуда.html>посу́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посудомойка.html>посудомо́йку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pósle obéda my <b>sostávim</b> posúdu v posudomójku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">After lunch we'll put the dishes in the dishwasher.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sostávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sostavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to constitute, to make up, to form
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>бо́льшую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тело.html>те́ла</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vodá <b>sostavljájet</b> bólʹšuju částʹ náševo téla.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Water <b>makes up</b> a majority of our bodies.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to compose, to construct, to draw up, to prepare
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:составить.html>соста́вить</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резюме.html>резюме́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak <b>sostávitʹ</b>/<b>sostavljátʹ</b> rezjumɛ́?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How should one prepare a résumé?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stack <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to place objects on top of each other to form a stack</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to transfer, to place <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to move things from one place to another</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:составлять.html>составля́ем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:посуда.html>посу́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посудомойка.html>посудомо́йку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pósle obéda my <b>sostavljájem</b> posúdu v posudomójku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">After lunch we put dishes into the dishwasher.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***состоятельный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:состоятельный.html>состоя́тельный</a> (13115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состоять.html>состоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sostojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состоятельный.html>состоя́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sostojátelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>affluent, wealthy, prosperous, well-off, well-to-do</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reasoned, persuasive, well-founded</li></ol>

***состоять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:состоять.html>состоя́ть</a> (1211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состоять.html>состоя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sostojátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive)
</p>
<ol><li>to consist (of)</li>
<li>to be a member of, to occupy a position, to be in a position, to belong to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чиновник.html>чино́вникам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:категория.html>катего́рии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:состоять.html>состоя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртии</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Po zakónu činóvnikam výsšej kategórii nelʹzjá <b>sostojátʹ</b> v pártii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">By law, the officials of the highest category cannot <b>belong</b> to a party.<br /><i>- Г. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зюганов: "<a href = vnd.unilang:спасение.html>Спасе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страны</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:советский.html>Сове́тская</a> Россия" 15 Jun 2003</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">consist of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складываться.html>скла́дываться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skládyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">consist of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional)</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</ol>

***сострадающий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сострадающий.html>сострада́ющий</a> (30043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
